// by the engine.\n127: type QueryLogger interface {\n128: \tslog.Handler\n129: \tio.Closer\n130: }\n131: \n132: // A Query is derived from a raw query string and can be run against an engine\n133: // If PromQL engine crashes while executing any query, such query should be present\n271: // in the tracker on restart, hence logged. After the logging on restart, the tracker gets emptied.\n272: //\n273: // 2) Enforcement of the maximum number of concurrent queries.\n274: type QueryTracker interface {\n275: \tio.Closer\n276: \n277: \t// GetMaxConcurrent returns maximum number of concurrent queries that are allowed by this tracker.\n278: \tGetMaxConcurrent() int\n279: \n280: \t// Insert inserts query into query tracker.
